### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="341" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="345" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="365" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="379" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="386" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="391" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="396" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="403" href="UALib.Algebras.html" class="Module">UALib.Algebras</a> <a id="418" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="424" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="425" href="UALib.Algebras.Signatures.html#1377" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="434" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="436" href="universes.html#613" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="437" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="439" href="universes.html#617" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="440" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="442" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="447" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="454" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html" class="Module">UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries</a> <a id="482" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="489" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="503" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="506" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="513" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">UALib.Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="539" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="540" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="544" href="UALib.Algebras.Signatures.html#1377" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="554" href="universes.html#613" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="556" href="universes.html#617" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="557" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="559" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#559" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="565" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="579" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="581" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="588" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="593" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="600" href="UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">UALib.Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="631" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="632" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="634" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="636" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="637" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="639" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#559" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="642" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="644" class="Keyword">public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2252" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2911" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="2927" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="2932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="2934" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2935" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2937" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="2939" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2941" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="2949" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="2951" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2951" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="2953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2955" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2961" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2969" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="2971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="2972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2975" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="2978" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="2979" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="2982" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="2985" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="2990" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2991" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="2999" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3000" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3002" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3004" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2937" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3005" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3007" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3008" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3011" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3014" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3016" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3018" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2937" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3019" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3022" class="Keyword">where</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3178" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3180" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3182" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3190" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="3192" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3193" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3195" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3197" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3161" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3199" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3201" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3202" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3203" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3204" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3211" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3213" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3178" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3215" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3471"   <a id="S.ssubw"></a><a id="3231" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3231" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="3237" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3239" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3240" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3242" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3242" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3244" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3246" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3254" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="3256" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3257" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3259" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3240" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3263" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3265" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3266" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3267" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2935" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3268" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3270" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2937" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3271" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3273" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2951" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3275" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3277" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3242" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3279" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3471" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="3281" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3240" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3283" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3242" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3287" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3289" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3291" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2951" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="S.siso"></a><a id="3295" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3295" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a>  <a id="3301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3303" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3304" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2951" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3627" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3632" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3634" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3635" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4161" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4122" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4163" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4165" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4122" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4167" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4171" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3651" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4175" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4175" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4182" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4184" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4185" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4185" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4187" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4187" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4189" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4191" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4199" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4201" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4202" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4206" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4185" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4208" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4210" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4211" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3635" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4213" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3637" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4216" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4218" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3651" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4220" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4222" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4185" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4224" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4226" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4187" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4228" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4230" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4187" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4232" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4234" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4236" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3651" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4576" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4581" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4583" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4584" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4586" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4588" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4590" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4598" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4602" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4604" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4610" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4618" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4620" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4621" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4623" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="4626" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4627" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4630" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="4633" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4638" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4639" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4648" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4650" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4652" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4653" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4655" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4656" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4658" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a><a id="4660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4661" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4663" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4665" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4666" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="4669" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="4677" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4677" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="4684" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4686" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4687" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4687" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4691" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4699" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4701" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4702" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4704" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4706" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4687" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4708" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4710" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4712" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4714" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#4395" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="4723" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4687" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4725" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4727" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4729" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4731" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5198" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5231" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5224" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5232" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5234" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5236" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5237" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5238" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5239" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5241" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5242" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5244" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5245" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5247" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5249" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5251" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5198" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5253" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5255" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5257" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5261" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5268" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5270" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5273" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5275" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5286" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5288" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5288" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5290" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5292" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5300" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5303" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5305" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5307" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5309" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5312" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5313" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5314" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5316" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5317" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5319" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5321" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5323" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5325" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5327" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5288" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5329" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5331" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5288" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5333" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5335" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5337" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5341" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5341" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5348" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5351" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5351" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5353" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5355" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5357" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5365" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5367" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5368" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5370" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5372" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5351" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5374" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5377" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5378" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4584" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5379" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5381" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5382" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5384" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5386" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5388" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5351" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5390" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5392" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5394" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5353" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5398" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5400" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5402" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4600" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5754" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5767" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5768" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5768" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5770" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5772" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5780" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5782" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5782" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5784" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5786" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5791" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5792" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5800" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5768" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5802" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5803" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5805" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5808" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5768" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5809" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5812" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5814" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5817" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5768" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5819" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5754" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5831" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5833" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5835" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5837" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5839" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5840" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5841" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5842" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5832" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5845" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5847" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5835" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5849" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5851" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5835" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5854" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5854" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5865" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5869" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5877" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5879" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5882" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5885" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5865" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5886" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5887" href="universes.html#527" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5889" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5854" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5899" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5901" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5903" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5905" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5905" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5907" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5910" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5916" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5899" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5926" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5927" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5929" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5932" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5899" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5933" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5936" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5938" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5754" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5949" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5905" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>




#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="6382" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6382" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6389" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6391" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6392" <a id="6775" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6382" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6782" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6782" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6787" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4175" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="6793" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6793" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6795" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="6797" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6799" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4175" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="6807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6808" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6382" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="6815" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6782" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="6819" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6793" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6820" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6822" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6795" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="7734" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7743" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7744" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7744" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7746" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7746" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="7748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7750" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="7758" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7760" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7762" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7767" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="7772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7773" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="7781" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7744" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="7783" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="7784" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7786" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="7789" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7744" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7790" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="7793" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7760" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7797" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7799" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="7802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="7805" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7806" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7744" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7807" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7809" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7746" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7810" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7760" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="7814" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="7816" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="7817" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7818" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7744" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="7819" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7821" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7746" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="7822" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7824" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="7828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7835" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7835" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7839" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7840" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7846" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7846" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7847" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="7860" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="7868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7869" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7835" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7873" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7846" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7874" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7876" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7883" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7888" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="7893" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7894" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7895" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7897" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7898" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="7908" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7924" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7883" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7928" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7897" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7929" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7931" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7938" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7938" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7943" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3152" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="7947" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7948" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7948" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7949" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7951" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7951" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7952" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7954" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7954" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7957" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7957" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7960" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="7963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7965" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3152" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="7970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7978" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7938" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="7982" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7954" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7984" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7986" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7957" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7990" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7997" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7997" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8002" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3231" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="8007" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8008" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8008" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="8009" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8011" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8011" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="8012" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8014" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8014" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="8017" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8017" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="8020" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8022" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8024" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3231" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="8030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8031" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8038" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7997" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8042" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8014" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="8044" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8046" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8017" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="8050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8057" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8057" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8062" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3295" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="8067" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8067" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8069" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8069" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="8071" class="Symbol">)</a>          <a id="8082" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8084" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3295" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="8089" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8090" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7734" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="8097" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8057" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="8101" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8067" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8102" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8104" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8069" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8316" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8316" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8329" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8331" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8332" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8332" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8334" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8334" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8338" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="8346" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8348" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8348" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8352" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8358" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8366" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8332" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8369" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8371" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8374" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8332" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8375" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="8378" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8378" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8382" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8390" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8391" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8332" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8393" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8395" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8334" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8396" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8399" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="8402" class="Symbol">→</a>             <a id="8416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8378" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8418" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3664" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8438" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8348" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="9985" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9988" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9990" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9902" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9992" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3664" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10012" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8763" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
   <a id="10017" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10020" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10022" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8801" class="Function">S→subalgebra</a> <a id="10035" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9905" class="Bound">sA</a>
   <a id="10041" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10041" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10044" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10046" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1409" class="Function">Subalgebra</a> <a id="10057" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10059" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10062" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10067" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10041" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10070" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10072" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11663" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="10076" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10078" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10081" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="10086" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10086" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10091" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10093" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9902" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10095" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="10097" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10099" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10041" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10102" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10107" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10086" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10112" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10114" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10118" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10120" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10124" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9985" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10127" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="lift-alg-subP"></a><a id="10411" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10411" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10425" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10427" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10428" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10430" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10430" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10434" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10442" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10444" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10444" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10448" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10454" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10462" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10464" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10465" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10467" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10470" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10471" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="10474" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10474" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10476" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10478" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10486" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10488" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10489" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="10492" class="Symbol">→</a>              <a id="10507" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10474" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10509" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3664" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10530" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10531" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10532" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10533" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10535" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10428" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10536" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10538" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10444" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10539" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="10671" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10411" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="10685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10686" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10686" The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

  <a id="12345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12324" class="Function">lAsp</a> <a id="12350" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12352" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8316" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a><a id="12364" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12365" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12106" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12367" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="12369" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12109" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12370" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12372" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12106" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="12374" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="12376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12109" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12377" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="12380" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12381" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12106" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="12382" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12384" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12109" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="12385" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12387" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12112" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12388" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12390" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12174" class="Function">lA</a><a id="12392" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12220" class="Function">lAsc</a>

  <a id="12402" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12402" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12174" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12412" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1114" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12115" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="12418" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12402" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12423" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12425" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4278" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="12433" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12174" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12436" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12115" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="12438" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12439" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2929" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="12445" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4843" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="12455" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12457" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12129" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="13318" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13318" class="Function">β</a> <a id="13320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13322" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Basic.html#2161" class="Function">is-homomorphism</a> <a id="13338" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13339" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13341" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13016" class="Function">SA</a><a id="13343" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13346" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13348" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12971" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13349" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13351" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13267" class="Function">α</a>
  <a id="13355" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13318" class="Function">β</a> <a id="13357" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13359" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13361" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13361" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13363" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13363" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13365" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13367" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#559" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="13371" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="13373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13373" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13375" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13378" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13382" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="13384" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13131" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="13389" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13373" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13391" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="13392" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13394" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13361" class="Bound">𝑓</a> <a id="13396" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13399" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13399" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13363" class="Bound">𝒂</a> <a id="13405" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13399" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13407" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13373" class="Bound">i</a><a id="13408" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13412" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13412" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13416" href="MGS-Embeddings.html#384" class="Function">is-embedding</a> <a id="13429" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13267" class="Function">α</a>
  <a id="13433" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13412" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="13435" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13437" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#10144" class="Function">embedding-lift</a> <a id="13452" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12902" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13456" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12902" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13460" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13461" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12907" class="Bound">I</a><a id="13462" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13464" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13016" class="Function">SA</a><a id="13466" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13468" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12971" class="Function">𝒜</a><a id="13469" class="Symbol">}</a><a id="13470" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13208" class="Function">h</a><a id="13471" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13474" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13474" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13476" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13478" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13480" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13131" class="Function">SA≤𝒜</a> <a id="13485" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13474" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13487" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="13488" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13493" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13493" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="13500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13502" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13504" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13016" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="13507" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3471" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="13509" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13511" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12971" class="Function">𝒜</a>
  <a id="13515" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13493" class="Function">⨅SA≤⨅𝒜</a> <a id="13522" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13525" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13267" class="Function">α</a> <a id="13527" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5665" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13529" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13318" class="Function">β</a><a id="13530" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13532" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5665" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13534" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13412" class="Function">γ</a>

  <a id="13539" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13539" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13543" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#1021" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="13545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12971" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="13547" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="13549" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="13551" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12899" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="13555" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13539" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="13557" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13559" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3929" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="13565" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13568" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13568" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13570" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13572" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6827" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="13579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13580" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="13582" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11744" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="13586" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13588" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12913" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="13592" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13568" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="13594" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11740" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="13596" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#11659" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="13597" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="13813" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13820" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13820" class="Module">_</a> <a id="13822" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="13825" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13827" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="13835" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="13837" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13837" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="13839" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13841" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="13846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13847" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="13855" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="13857" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="13858" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13860" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13864" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13867" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13868" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13874" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="13882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13883" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13886" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13887" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13889" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="13892" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13823" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="13893" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="13896" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="13904" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13904" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="13908" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13910" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15400" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15361" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15404"  <a id="15751" class="Symbol">→</a>     <a id="15757" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="15758" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15759" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15704" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15761" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15763" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15706" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15764" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15766" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15704" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15768" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15770" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15706" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15771" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15773" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15774" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15775" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15776" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15704" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15777" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15779" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15706" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15780" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15782" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15720" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="15783" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15785" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3014" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="15787" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4581" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="15788" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15789" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15704" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15790" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="15792" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15706" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="15793" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15720" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="15798" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15696" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="15809" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15810" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15810" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="15811" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15813" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15813" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="15818" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15820" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15822" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15354" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="15826" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4175" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="15833" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15813" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="15839" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4843" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="15849" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15851" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15696" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15856" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15857" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3087" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="15862" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15863" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15863" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="15864" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15866" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15866" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15867" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15869" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4801" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="15878" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15879" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15696" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="15884" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#15866" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15885" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove the result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="16524" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16524" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="16542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16545" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16547" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16549" href="universes.html#551" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="16557" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16559" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16559" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16561" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16563" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16565" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="16566" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16568" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16568" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16570" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16572" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1071" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16577" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16578" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#771" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16586" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="16588" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#540" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16589" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16591" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16594" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16595" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="16599" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="16618" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#4048" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="16632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16633" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16634" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16636" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16637" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16639" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16559" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16640" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16643" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="16645" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16568" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16646" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16648" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2732" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="16650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16651" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3632" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="16652" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16653" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16656" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16657" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16659" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#2030" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16662" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16545" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16663" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16666" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2932" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="16668" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16568" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16669" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="16673" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16524" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="16691" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16692" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16692" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="16693" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16695" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16695" class="Bound">X</a><a id="16696" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16698" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16698" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="16699" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="16702" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16704" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4095" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="16710" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#16978" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="16717" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16718" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6702" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="16721" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#559" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="16725" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17029" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="16730" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="16733" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="17144" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
